      " data-qa="headline">Jacinda Ardern, feted as ‘the anti-Trump,’ is poised to win New Zealand election</h1></div></header><article class="grid-item grid-item--cols-sm-12 grid-item--cols-md-12 b-l br-l mb-xxl-ns mt-xxs mt-md-l grid-item--cols-lg-8 pr-lg-lg" data-qa="main"><figure class="center mb-md ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter ml-auto-ns mr-auto-ns  overflow-hidden relative hide-for-print"><div style="filter:blur(10px);transition:filter .1s" class="w-100 mw-100 h-auto" width="600" height="899"><img src="https://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-apps/imrs.php?src=https://arc-anglerfish-washpost-prod-washpost.s3.amazonaws.com/public/46ZDVGADIMI6XCL5HJRADVTEH4.jpg&amp;w=32" alt="New Zealand Prime Minister Jacinda Ardern speaks at a September conference in Auckland ahead of the country’s elections." class="w-100 mw-100 h-auto" width="600" height="899"/></div><figcaption class="left ml-gutter mr-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns gray-dark font--subhead font-xxxs mt-xs mb-sm" aria-hidden="true">New Zealand Prime Minister Jacinda Ardern speaks at a September conference in Auckland ahead of the country’s elections. (Hannah Peters/Getty Images)</figcaption></figure><div class="flex"><div class="items-center"><div class="byline flex mb-sm" data-qa="byline"><div class="dib gray-dark font--subhead self-center author-text font-xxs"><div class="author-names"><span>By </span><span data-qa="author-name-wrapper"><span class="author-name font-bold black">Emanuel Stoakes</span></span></div></div></div><div class="mb-md gray-dark font--subhead font-xxs" data-qa="timestamp"><div class="display-date">October 12, 2020 at 5:00 AM EDT</div></div></div></div><div class="article-body"><div class="teaser-content"><section><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">CHRISTCHURCH, New Zealand — No leader of New Zealand has possessed a profile like Jacinda Ardern's. Her image has been <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FwHjWq6ONF0" title="www.youtube.com">projected onto the world's tallest building</a>, <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/feb/21/a-new-kind-of-soft-power-jacinda-ardern-appears-on-cover-of-time-magazine" title="www.theguardian.com">made the cover of Time magazine</a> and reached an audience that far exceeds her country's modest population.</p></div><div><div class="db dn-ns b bh bc-gray-lighter mb-md mr-neg-gutter ml-neg-gutter hide-for-print" data-qa="subscribe-promo"><a class="pt-sm pb-sm flex justify-center items-center bold font-xxxs" href="https://subscribe.washingtonpost.com/acq/#/offers/promo/o24_ma" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" style="border:none;color:#166dfc"><span class="mr-xs">Support our journalism. Subscribe today.</span><svg class="content-box  " width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="fill:#166dfc" data-sc-v="3.11.0" data-sc-c="icon"><title data-sc-v="3.11.0" data-sc-c="icon">arrow-right</title><path d="M7.664 1.25l6 6a1 1 0 010 1.414l-6 6L6.25 13.25 10.499 9H2V7h8.585L6.25 2.664 7.664 1.25z" fill-rule="nonzero" data-sc-v="3.11.0" data-sc-c="icon"></path></svg></a></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Feted by progressives globally for compassionate and decisive responses to crises, she earned the nickname “<a href="https://www.vogue.com/article/jacinda-ardern-new-zealand-prime-minister-vogue-march-2018-issue" title="www.vogue.com">the anti-Trump</a>” for her embrace of multilateralism and liberal values.</p></div></section></div><div class="remainder-content"><section><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Ardern is on course to comfortably win a second term in elections Oct. 17, with her Labour Party holding a <a href="https://www.rnz.co.nz/news/political/427898/election-2020-labour-steady-national-down-in-latest-poll" title="www.rnz.co.nz">double-digit lead</a> over conservative National in surveys. Yet her record is more complicated than her reputation suggests, and the surge in her domestic popularity is a relatively recent phenomenon that will be tested amid a deep recession and against circumstances unprecedented in living memory.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“There has always been a lot of goodwill toward Ardern at home, but much less than abroad,” said political analyst Josh Van Veen, noting that her personal support was below 40 percent late last year. “It looked as though she was on course to be a one-term prime minister. Then, covid-19 turned everyone’s world upside down.”</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Indeed, crisis has defined Ardern’s premiership: a <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/brenton-tarrant-sentence-life-prison-new-zealand-christchurch-mosque-shooting/2020/08/26/ddb9dc2a-e76a-11ea-bf44-0d31c85838a5_story.html?itid=lk_inline_manual_9" title="www.washingtonpost.com">massacre of 51 Muslim worshipers</a> by a white supremacist in Christchurch; a deadly <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/new-zealand-needed-human-skin-to-treat-volcano-burn-victims-help-came-from-ohio/2019/12/13/9e8dbdf2-1cf7-11ea-977a-15a6710ed6da_story.html?itid=lk_inline_manual_9" title="www.washingtonpost.com">volcano eruption</a>; and the coronavirus pandemic. Each time, Ardern, 40, won plaudits for her actions — leading the nation in mourning and tightening gun laws, <a href="https://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=12292678" title="www.nzherald.co.nz">hugging first responders</a> after the volcano disaster, and leading a <a href="https://www.health.govt.nz/our-work/diseases-and-conditions/covid-19-novel-coronavirus/covid-19-current-situation/covid-19-current-cases" title="www.health.govt.nz">pandemic response</a> widely hailed as among the world’s most effective.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">But Ardern’s progress has been limited on other goals, such as tackling a housing shortage and high rates of child poverty. Labour pledged to build 100,000 houses in a decade but <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/sep/04/new-zealand-scraps-overly-ambitious-plan-to-tackle-housing-crisis" title="www.theguardian.com">dropped the target</a> last year, having built 258 up to that point. <a href="https://wellbeingindicators.stats.govt.nz/en/income-inequality/" title="wellbeingindicators.stats.govt.nz">Income inequality</a> and levels of <a href="https://www.stats.govt.nz/information-releases/child-poverty-statistics-year-ended-june-2019" title="www.stats.govt.nz">material hardship for children</a> are little changed, official data show.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_2"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_2"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Meanwhile, defeating the virus has come at great cost: New Zealand’s economy <a href="https://www.stats.govt.nz/indicators/gross-domestic-product-gdp" title="www.stats.govt.nz">shrank by 12.2 percent</a> in the second quarter, nearly double the contraction in neighboring Australia.</p></div><div><p><span data-qa="interstitial-link-wrapper" class="font--body font-copy hide-for-print ma-0 pb-md db  italic interstitial"><a data-qa="interstitial-link" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/new-zealand-coronavirus-election-jacinda-ardern/2020/08/16/2366c508-e02c-11ea-82d8-5e55d47e90ca_story.html?itid=lk_interstitial_manual_14">New Zealand leader Jacinda Ardern delays election due to coronavirus outbreak</a></span></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">The conditions worry Mark Adams, 57, a sheep and cattle farmer from Fairlie, on New Zealand’s South Island, who says he will not vote for Labour.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“Even the most grizzled farmer would concede she’s done a good job on many issues,” he said, citing Ardern’s handling of the pandemic. “Without healthy people, you don’t have an economy, but it’s not kumbaya either,” he added, saying he felt National was better placed to fight the recession.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">More than six months of border restrictions have hammered tourism operators. “Pre-covid-19, tourism in New Zealand was a $112 million-per-day industry. We are already losing $47 million a day from [the absence of] international visitors,” said a spokesperson for Tourism Industry Aotearoa, quoting figures in New Zealand dollars. (The figures in U.S. dollars are $73.8 million and $30.9 million, respectively.)</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_3"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_3"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Van Veen expects the recession to have a profound impact on the national psyche. “Most New Zealanders have never experienced genuine hardship before. That could be about to change,” he said.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Ardern’s office declined to comment on the election, saying she was focused on the <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/coronavirus/?itid=lk_inline_manual_21" target="_blank" class="contextual_link">coronavirus</a> and would not consider international media requests.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">That is a shift for Ardern, who previously <a href="https://www.vogue.com/article/jacinda-ardern-new-zealand-prime-minister-vogue-march-2018-issue" title="www.vogue.com">posed for Vogue</a> and hosted comedian Stephen Colbert at her Auckland home. She even <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=DUPo62ouU84&amp;list=PLZMTrPGpJ8OCJSC4FJJgoJw3NcieXpnnv&amp;ab_channel=TheLateShowwithStephenColbert" title="www.youtube.com">picked him up from the airport</a>.</p></div><div><h3 class="font--subhead gray-darkest ma-0 pb-sm pt-lgmod">A roller-coaster term</h3></div><div><div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Ardern spent nine years as a lesser-known lawmaker before rising to national prominence in February 2017 when she won a by-election for Auckland’s Mount Albert  seat. Within months, she was promoted to deputy and then leader of Labour. An inconclusive general election later that year led her to enter a sometimes-awkward ruling coalition with right-leaning populist partner New Zealand First and the left-wing Green Party.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_4"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_4"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">New Zealanders do not directly elect the prime minister but vote for parties and local representatives. The share of seats allotted to a party is determined by its overall vote.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">As prime minister, Ardern pledged to redress long-standing social issues, <a href="https://www.newshub.co.nz/home/election/2017/10/homelessness-proves-capitalism-is-a-blatant-failure-jacinda-ardern.html" title="www.newshub.co.nz">making waves</a> by describing capitalism as a “blatant failure” from the perspective of poor New Zealanders. “What is the point of economic growth when we have some of the worst homelessness in the developed world?” she asked her interviewer.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Then, a major test came on March 15, 2019, when a gunman opened fire at two Christchurch mosques, shocking a nation unaccustomed to extremist violence.</p></div><div><p><span data-qa="interstitial-link-wrapper" class="font--body font-copy hide-for-print ma-0 pb-md db  italic interstitial"><a data-qa="interstitial-link" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2020/09/21/new-zealand-an-early-success-story-set-ease-most-restrictions-once-again-second-outbreak-slows/?itid=lk_interstitial_manual_31">New Zealand eases most restrictions as second virus outbreak slows</a></span></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Under the glare of the world’s media, Ardern led the mourning, showing solidarity with Muslims by <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/mar/28/with-respect-how-jacinda-ardern-showed-the-world-what-a-leader-should-be" title="www.theguardian.com">wearing a headscarf</a> as she consoled grieving relatives. Her subsequent changes to gun laws, including a <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/new-zealand-passes-law-banning-most-semiautomatic-weapons-less-than-a-month-after-mosque-massacres/2019/04/10/38e2c202-5b6b-11e9-b8e3-b03311fbbbfe_story.html?itid=lk_inline_manual_32" title="www.washingtonpost.com">ban on semiautomatic weapons</a>, were approved within weeks with near-unanimous support.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“We feel deeply in our hearts what has happened to you. We feel grief. We feel injustice. We feel anger. And we share that with you,” she told members of the Muslim community.</p></div><div><div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Her empathy was <a href="https://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=12292678" title="www.nzherald.co.nz">again on display</a> after the White Island volcano erupted last December, killing 21 people, and during the coronavirus pandemic, when her swift decision to institute a lockdown helped New Zealand <a href="https://www.health.govt.nz/our-work/diseases-and-conditions/covid-19-novel-coronavirus/covid-19-current-situation/covid-19-current-cases" title="www.health.govt.nz">beat back the virus</a>. A second wave in August spurred a tightening of controls, but since then, the country has largely returned to normal.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_5"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_5"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">As restrictions were imposed earlier this year, Ardern called on New Zealanders to “save lives by staying home” and later congratulated the “team of 5 million” for subduing the threat by observing the rules.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">To many, Ardern represented something else: a counterpoint to the populism that has jolted the United States and Europe.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Indeed, Ardern has had an uneasy relationship with President Trump. When Trump said at a diplomatic dinner in 2017 that Ardern had “caused a lot of upset in her country,” Ardern <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2017/nov/17/jacinda-ardern-to-donald-trump-no-one-marched-when-i-was-elected" title="www.theguardian.com">retorted,</a> “No one marched when I was elected.”</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">More recently, she <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/aug/21/very-proud-jacinda-ardern-defends-new-zealand-covid-response-after-trump-attacks" title="www.theguardian.com">rebuked Trump</a> when he suggested New Zealand was struggling with its second virus outbreak, pointing out that her nation’s new cases, then averaging about nine a day, paled in comparison with the number in the United States. New Zealand’s virus fatality rate is 0.5 per 100,000 population, compared with 66 in the United States, according to <a href="https://coronavirus.jhu.edu/data/mortality" title="coronavirus.jhu.edu">data from Johns Hopkins University</a>.</p></div><div><h3 class="font--subhead gray-darkest ma-0 pb-sm pt-lgmod">More than a pandemic</h3></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">As the election nears, Labour has again promised higher minimum wages and extended sick-pay entitlements, building on measures to increase support to lower-income voters.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_6"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_6"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">But some want greater action on entrenched problems that disproportionately affect New Zealand’s indigenous Maori community.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“I understand why she hasn’t been able to do more in her first term, but despite these dynamics, my people are still suffering, they are still more likely to be broke, imprisoned, to be discriminated against, to go hungry than other groups,” said Matthew Tukaki, executive director of the New Zealand Maori Council. “Nothing has really changed for us; this election can’t just be about covid.”</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">From the left, there has been criticism that Ardern has underwhelmed on climate change, despite banning new offshore oil and gas exploration.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_7"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“Deep-sea oil permits are still being handed out, and the increase in intensive farming practices is definitely a step in the wrong direction,” said Claire Dann, a neighbor of Adams in Fairlie.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_7"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">And on foreign policy, Ardern has faced accusations of timidity in the face of China’s growing aggression, including evidence of malevolent actions by the Chinese Communist Party on New Zealand soil.</p></div><div><p><span data-qa="interstitial-link-wrapper" class="font--body font-copy hide-for-print ma-0 pb-md db  italic interstitial"><a data-qa="interstitial-link" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/china-new-zealand-jacinda-ardern-xi-jinping/2020/07/05/f8d5e182-af95-11ea-98b5-279a6479a1e4_story.html?itid=lk_interstitial_manual_53">Under Jacinda Ardern, New Zealand pivots on how to deal with China</a></span></p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">The election will be held in conjunction with two referendums, on <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/10/01/world/asia/jacinda-ardern-cannabis-new-zealand.html" title="www.nytimes.com">whether to legalize marijuana</a> and whether to allow euthanasia for the terminally ill. Ardern and most of her party have backed euthanasia, but she has declined to say where she stands on marijuana, despite admitting in a televised debate that she smoked the drug “a long time ago.”</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print db dn-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_mob_bigbox_8"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">On Sept. 9, Ardern relaunched her campaign — the election was <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/new-zealand-coronavirus-election-jacinda-ardern/2020/08/16/2366c508-e02c-11ea-82d8-5e55d47e90ca_story.html?itid=lk_inline_manual_56" title="www.washingtonpost.com">postponed for four weeks</a> because of the pandemic — with a <a href="https://www.instagram.com/tv/CE5AIMWHtBT/?utm_source=ig_web_copy_link" title="www.instagram.com">message on Instagram</a> posted from a van near her hometown of Morrinsville, where Ardern’s parents were babysitting her daughter.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“Have a beautiful day, wherever you are,” she said cheerily. Her performance during televised debates has been similarly upbeat and composed, despite a strong challenge from Judith Collins, the opposition leader.</p></div><div><div class="cb bg-offwhite mt-xxs pt-md pb-md mb-lg ml-neg-gutter mr-neg-gutter mr-auto-ns ml-auto-ns hide-for-print dn db-ns relative" data-qa="article-body-ad" style="min-height:250px"><div class="absolute z-0" aria-hidden="true" style="left:50%;top:50%">AD</div><div class="relative z-1"><div class=""><wp-ad class="hide-for-print  hide-for-print" id="slug_inline_bb_8"></wp-ad></div></div></div></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">Patrick Lee-Lo, 62, a small-business owner from Auckland, said he had not voted for Ardern because she was “too inexperienced in business,” but he was still impressed, particularly by her “love, kindness and empathy” after the Christchurch attacks.</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md ">“One thing covid has taught me, and the world, is you can no longer take things for granted,” he said. “Right now, most decent people are likely to respond to those leaders who make them feel cared about.”</p></div><div><p class="font--body font-copy gray-darkest ma-0 pb-md bold"> </p></div><div><p><span data-qa="interstitial-link-wrapper" class="font--body font-copy hide-for-print ma-0 pb-md db "><a
